 is pitishan ko austrailia kii rahane vaali Katrina Collins ne taiyaar kiya tha
 Because abusive messages were written on this messaging app platform for their daughter
 apni 13 varshiya beti ko is plateform par mili bhadde caments ke baad Katrina Collins neikehange
 Created a petition on org
 isamen colins ne ap ko bain karne kii maang rakhi

 Now it cannot be downloaded from here
 haalanki jin logon ne pehle se is ap ko install kiya hua he wo ise istemaal karnaa jari rakh sakate hai

 launch ke saath hi isaki lokapriyata ne ap ko duniyabar main mashhoor kar diya

 Prior to his work as an actor, he used to do petty jobs, also driving vehicles
 us jamaane main minaa kumari ko teble tennis sikhaane ke liye unhen naukari par rakhaa gaya tha
 He later married Meena Kumari's sister Madhu
 shaadi karne or pita banane ke baad zyada paise kamaane ke liye unhone abhinay karne kaa nishchay kiya
 Initially, he played minor roles in films like 'do Bigha Zameen' and 'pyaasa'
 mahmud ko filmon main pehla bada mauka 'parvarish' (1958) se mila tha
 In this, he played the role of the brother of the film's hero Raj Kapoor and after that he also acted in the film 'gumnaam'
 unhone 'pyaar kiye ja', 'pyaar hi pyaar', 'sasuraal', 'lav in tokyo' or 'ziddee' jaisi hit filmein di
 He then went on to play the lead role in a few films, but the audience liked him more as a comedian
 mahmud ne baad main apana khud kaa production house kholaa
 His first home production film was 'chhote Nawab'
 unhone bataur nirdeshak suspence-kamedi film 'bhoot bangla' banaai
 Mahmood, who worked as an actor, director, narrator and producer, made his last film 'dushman Duniya Ka' in 1996 with Shah Rukh Khan, but failed at the box office
 apni chhavi main ai ekarupata se bachane ke liye mahmud ne apane aap ko vibhinn prakaar kii bhoomikaaon main pesh kiya
 In the same sequence, in the year 1968, the name of the film 'padosan' comes first
 'padosan' main mahmud ne nakaaratmak bhoomika nibhaai or darshakon kii vaahvahee luutane main safal rahe
 'padosan' was a tremendous hit of the 60s
 'padosan' ko hindi cinema jagat kii shreshth hasya filmon main gina jaataa he
 He appeared heavily on the character of the hero in many of his films
 'padosan' main mahmud par filmaaya gaanaa 'ek chatur naar karke shringaar' kaaphi lokapriy hua
 In the 1970 film Humjoli, the audience got to see various forms of acting of Mahmood
 is film main mahmud ne tihari bhoomika nibhaai or darshakon kaa dhyaan apni ore khinchaa
 The comments mahmud ko apane sine kariyar main teen baar filmphere puraskaar se sammanit kiya gaya
 On 23 July 2004, Mahmud departed from this world forever and only his beautiful memories remain among us

 ) If Mahmood's acting car started, then films like 'bhoot Bangla', 'padosan', 'bombay to Goa', 'gumnaam', 'kunvara Bap' established Mahmood
 mahmud apni alag adaa ke liye logon ke chahete ban gaye, na sirf filmi duniya ke liye, balki apane prashansakon ke liye bhi
 Mehmood was born on September 29, 1932 in Mumbai
 unke pita mumtaj ali bombai tokies studio main kaam karte the
 To meet the economic needs of the house, Mahmud sold toffees in local trains running between Malad and Virar
 bachapan ke dinon se hi mahmud kaa rujhaan abhinay main tha
 In 1943 he got a chance to try his luck in the Bombay Talkies film 'kismat' because of his father's recommendation
 film main mahmud ne abhinayta ashok kumaar ke bachapan kii bhoomika nibhaai thi
 In the language of Mahmud, the Hyderabadi style was liked by the audience and the great style of his speaking and acting made millions of people crazy
 mahmud ne jis vakt filmon ko gambhirtha se lenaa shuru kiya tha, us samay bhartiya film jagat main kishor kumaar kii kamedi kaa jaadu chaaya hua tha
 Writer Manmohan Melville has narrated an interesting anecdote of Mahmood and Kishore in one of his articles
 isamen kaha gaya he ki mahmud ne apane kariyar ke sunahare daur se guzar rahe kishor se apni kisi film main bhoomika dene kii guzarish kii thi, lekin mahmud kii pratibha se puri tarah waakif kishor ne kaha tha ki vah aise kisi vyakti ko mauka kaise de sakate hai, jo bhavishya main unheen ke liye chunauti ban jaae
 On this, Mahmud said with great humility that one day i will also become a big filmmaker and will give you a role in my film
 mahmud apni baat ke pakke sabit hue or aage chalakar jab unhone apni home production kii film 'padosan' shuru kii to usamen kishor ko kaam diya
 The film proved to be Bollywood's biggest comedy film due to the jugalbandi of both these great actors
 mahmud ke teen dashak lambey kariyar main 300 se zyada hindi filmein unke naam hai
 Mahmood was one of the eight children of actor and dance artist Mumtaz Ali
 abhinayta ke taur par kaam se pehle vah chote-mote kaam karte the, vaahan chalaane kaa kaam bhi karte the
 At that time, Meena Kumari was hired to teach table tennis
 baad main unhone minaa kumari kii bahan madhu se shaadi kii
 After marrying and becoming a father, he decided to pursue acting to earn more money
 shuruyaat main unhone 'do bigha jameen' or 'pyaasa' jaisi filmon main chote-mote kirdaar nibhaae
 Mehmood got his first big chance in films with 'parvarish' (1958)
 isamen unhone film ke nayak rajkpur ke bhai kaa kirdaar nibhaayaa tha or uske baad unhone film 'gumnaam' main bhi kaam kiya
 He gave hits like 'pyar Kiya Jaa', 'pyar Hi Pyar', 'sasural', 'love in Tokyo' and 'stubborn'
 iske baad unhone kuch filmon main mukhya bhoomika bhi nibhaai, lekin darshakon ne unhen ek kamedian ke taur par zyada pasand kiya
 Mahmud later opened his own production house
 unki pehali home production film 'chote nawab' thi
 He made the suspense-comedy film Bhoot Bangla as a director
 abhinayta, nirdeshak, kathakaar or nirmaataa ke rup main kaam karne vaale mahmud ne shahrukh khan ko lekar varsh 1996 main apni aakhri film 'dushman duniya kaa' banaai, lekin vah box offis par naakaam rahi
 To avoid uniformity in his image, Mahmood introduced himself in a wide variety of roles
 isi kram main varsh 1968 main film 'padosan' kaa naam sabase pehle aata he
 In 'padosan', Mahmood played a negative role and managed to rob the applause of the audience
 'padosan' 60 ke dashak kii jabardast hit sabit hui thi
 'padosan' is counted among the best comedy films of the Hindi cinema world
 apni anek filmon main vah nayak ke kirdaar par baari najar aae
 The song 'ek Chatur Nar Karkar Shringar', which was filmed on Mehmood in 'padosan', became very popular
 1970 main film 'hamajoli' main mahmud ke abhinay ke vividh rup darshakon ko dekhne ko mili
 In this film, Mahmood played a triple role and caught the attention of the audience
 tippaniyan Mehmood was awarded the Filmfare Award thrice in his cine career
 23 july, 2004 ko mahmud is duniya se hameshaa ke liye chale gaye or hamaare bich keval unki khubasurat yaaden hi baaki hai

 ) mahmud kaa janm 29 sitambar, 1932 ko mumbai main hua tha
 His father Mumtaz Ali used to work at Bombay Talkies Studio
 ghar kii aarthik jaruratein puri karne ke liye mahmud, malad or viraar ke bich chalane vaali local trainon main toffiyaan bechaa karte the
 Since childhood, Mahmud was in acting
 pita kii sifarish kii vajah se 1943 main unhen bombai tokies kii film 'kismat' main kismat aajamaane kaa mauka mila
 In the film, Mahmood played the childhood role of actor Ashok Kumar
 mahmud kii bhashaa main hyderaabadi andaaj darshakon ko behad pasand aayaa or unke bolne kii kala or abhinay ke laajawab andaaj ne karodon logon ko apana divaana bana liya
 At the time when Mahmud started taking films seriously, Kishore Kumar's comedy was overshadowed in the Indian film industry
 lekhak manmohan melville ne apane ek lekh main mahmud or kishor ke dilachasp kisse ko bayaan kiya he
 It said that Mahmood had requested Kishore, who is going through the golden phase of his career, to play a role in one of his films, but Kishore, who was fully aware of Mahmood's talent, said that how can he give such a chance to someone Which will become a challenge for them in the future
 is par mahmud ne badi vinamrata ke saath kaha ki ek din main bhi bada filmkaar banuunga or aapako apni film main bhoomika duungaa
 Mehmood proved his point and later when he started his home production film 'padosan', he hired Kishore in it
